(j // (threads_per_head * vs)) * vs\n        return thread_id, local_id\n\n    @T.prim_func\n    def engram_gate_bwd_kernel(\n        grad_out: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        gate_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_x_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_k_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        grad_x: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_k: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_v: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_w_partial: T.Tensor[(num_persistent_blocks, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.float],\n    ):\n        with T.Kernel(num_persistent_blocks, threads=threads) as pid_p:\n            tid = T.get_thread_binding()\n            warp_id = T.get_warp_idx()\n            lane_id = T.get_lane_idx()\n            head_id = warp_id // warps_per_head\n            sub_warp_id = warp_id % warps_per_head\n\n            go_local = T.alloc_local((go_vec_size,), T.float)\n            v_local = T.alloc_local((go_vec_size,), T.float)\n            go_v_local = T.alloc_local((v_vec_size,), T.float)\n            go_x_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            x_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            k_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            w_fused_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            grad_v_partial = T.alloc_local((v_vec_size,), T.float)\n            grad_w_local = T.alloc_local((elems_per_warp_pair,), T.float)\n\n            dldg_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            dldg_r = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n\n            gate_local = T.alloc_local((hc_mult,), T.float)\n            gate_local_hc = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            rstd_x_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            rstd_k_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_in_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_x_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_k_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n\n            go_copy_layout = T.Fragment((hc_mult, go_blk_d), forward_fn=partial(smem_layout, vs=go_vec_size))\n            x_copy_layout = T.Fragment((hc_mult, x_blk_d), forward_fn=partial(smem_layout, vs=x_vec_size))\n\n            go_smem = T.alloc_shared((hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16)\n            v_smem = T.alloc_shared((hidden_size,), T.bfloat16)\n            x_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n            k_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n            w_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.float)\n            dldg_smem = T.alloc_shared((hc_mult, warps_per_head), T.float)\n\n            per_block = T.ceildiv(num_tokens, num_persistent_blocks)\n            t_start = T.min(per_block * pid_p, num_tokens)\n            t_end = T.min(per_block * (pid_p + 1), num_tokens)\n\n            T.clear(grad_w_local)\n\n            for i_s in T.serial(t_start, t_end):\n                # === Prologue: load grad_out and v into smem ===\n                if i_s == t_start:\n                    T.async_copy(v[i_s, :], v_smem)\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s, :, :go_blk_d], go_smem[:, :go_blk_d],       rstd_k_local = rstd_k_in[i_s, head_id]\n                dot_in_local = dot_in[i_s, head_id]\n\n                T.clear(dldg_local)\n\n                go_sub_blks = go_blk_d // (threads_per_head * go_vec_size)\n                num_go_tiles = hidden_size // go_blk_d\n\n                # === Pass 1a: dldg — two warps per head ===\n                for i_b in T.serial(1, num_go_tiles):\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s, :, i_b * go_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * go_blk_d],\n                                 go_smem[:, i_b * go_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * go_blk_d],\n                                 loop_layout=go_copy_layout)\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(1)\n                    for i_sub in T.serial(go_sub_blks):\n                        go_base = (i_b - 1) * go_blk_d + i_sub * threads_per_head * go_vec_size + sub_warp_id * warp_size * go_vec_size\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(go_vec_size):\n                            go_local[i_k] = go_smem[head_id,                 dldg_local[0] += go_local[i_k] * v_local[i_k]\n\n                # Epilogue: process last go tile\n                T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n                for i_sub in T.serial(go_sub_blks):\n                    go_base = (num_go_tiles - 1) * go_blk_d + i_sub * threads_per_head * go_vec_size + sub_warp_id * warp_size * go_vec_size\n                    for i_k in              dldg_r[0] = T.Select(\n                    T.abs(dot_in_local) * scalar * rstd_x_local * rstd_k_local < clamp_value,\n                    0.0,\n                    dldg_r[0] * (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # Vector size for memory coalescing\n    VEC_SIZE = 8\n    \n    # Grid: one program per (token, head)\n    grid = (num_tokens, hc_mult)\n    \n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states,\n        k,\n        v,\n        weight_fused,\n        output,\n        dot_out,\n        gate_score,\n        rstd_x,\n        rstd_k,\n        num_tokens=num_tokens,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_H=hc_mult,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D=BLOCK_SIZE_D,\n        VEC_SIZE=VEC_SIZE,\n        num_warps=8,\n        num_stages=3,\n    )\n    \n    return output, dot_out, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n"},"output":"Wrote file successfully.","metadata":{"diagnostics":{},"filepath":"/app/engram_triton.py","exists":true,"truncated":false},"title":"app/engram_triton.py","time":{"start":1784533386731,"end":1784533386747}},"id":"prt_f7e7a2b13001U0XEa2qWJ3y4mt","sessionID":"ses_081861573ffewpFS5uHIUjBEpO","messageID":"msg_f7e7a2194001paMdQeKa4gGGDN"}}

Load data\n            x = tl.load(hs_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            v = tl.load(v_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            \n            # Compute output: x + gate * v\n            out = x + gate * v\n            \n            # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # Allocate outputs\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot_out = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot_out = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    \n    # Tune block size based on hidden_size\n    if hidden_size >= 7168:\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D = 1024\n    elif hidden_size >= 4096:\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D = 512\n    else:\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D = 256\n    \n    # First pass: compute reduction stats with vectorized loads\n        for d_start in range(0, hidden_size, BLOCK_SIZE_D):\n            d_offs = d_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE_D)\n            mask = d_offs < hidden_size\n            \n            # Load data as bf16, convert to float32\n            x = tl.load(hs_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            k = tl.load(k_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            w = tl.load(w_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            \n            # Fused multiply-add for better precision and performance\n            xk = x * k\n            sum_x2 += tl.sum(x * x, axis=0)\n            sum_k2 += tl.sum(k * k, axis=0)\n            sum_xwk += tl.sum(xk * w, axis=0)\n        \n        # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # Allocate outputs\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot_out = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot_out = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    \n    # Tune block size and tokens per block based on hidden_size\n    # For hidden_size=4096, use larger blocks for better memory coalescing\n    if hidden_size >= 7168:\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D = 1024\n        NUM_TOKENS_PER_BLOCK = 64\n    elif hidden_size >= 4096:\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D = 1024\n        NUM_TOKENS_PER_BLOCK = 64\n    else:\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D = 512\n        NUM_TOKENS_PER_BLOCK = 128\n    \n    # Persistent kernel: each block processes multiple tokens for one head\n    num_blocks = (num_tokens + NUM_TOKENS_PER_BLOCK - 1) // NUM_TOKENS_PER_BLOCK\n    \n    # Grid: (hc_mult, num_blocks)\n    grid = (hc_mult, num_blocks)\n    \n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states,\n        k,\n        v,\n        weight_fused,\n        output,\n        dot_out,\n        gate_score,\n        rstd_x,\n        rstd_k,\n        num_tokens=num_tokens,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D=BLOCK_SIZE_D,\n        NUM_TOKENS_PER_BLOCK=NUM_TOKENS_PER_BLOCK,\n        num_warps=8,\n        num_stages=5,\n    )\n    \n    return output, dot_out, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n"},"output":"Wrote file successfully.","metadata":{"diagnostics":{},"filepath":"/app/engram_triton.py","exists":true,"truncated":false},"title":"app/engram_triton.py","time":{"start":1784533677705,"end":1784533677710}},"id":"prt_f7e7ea54b0016rvLPk80JujpQG","sessionID":"ses_081861573ffewpFS5uHIUjBEpO","messageID":"msg_f7e7e8b1e0014dJNv27hgrKbwl"}}

{"type":"tool_use","timestamp":1784533722107,"sessionID":"ses_081861573ffewpFS5uHIUjBEpO","part":{"type":"tool","tool":"write","callID":"call_c77e0094b7be48d392aa7129","state":{"status":"completed","input":{"filePath":"/app/engram_triton.py","content":"\"\"\"Implement the Engram gate forward pass as a Triton kernel.\n\nFill in `engram_gate_fwd_triton` with a real Triton kernel. The grader\nimports THIS function and compares it against both the PyTorch reference and the\nDeepSeek TileLang kernel for correctness, then times it against the TileLang\nkernel for speedup.\n\nDo NOT change the function name or signature.\n\"\"\"\nimport torch\nimport triton\nimport triton.language as tl\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef _engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    hidden_states_ptr,\n    k_ptr,\n    v_ptr,\n    weight_fused_ptr,\n    output_ptr,\n    dot_out_ptr,\n    gate_score_ptr,\n    rstd_x_ptr,\n    rstd_k_ptr,\n    num_tokens: tl.constexpr,\n    hc_mult: tl.constexpr,\n    hidden_size: tl.constexpr,\n    eps: tl.constexpr,\n    scalar: tl.constexpr,\n    clamp_value: tl.constexpr,\n    save_for_backward: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_SIZE_D: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward kernel optimized for AMD MI350.\n    \n    Each program handles one (token, head) pair.\n    Uses large block size for efficient memory access.\n    \"\"\"\n    pid_token = tl.program_id(0)\n    pid_head = tl.program_id(1)\n    \n    if pid_token >= num_tokens:\n        return\n    \n    # Base offsets for this (token, head)\n    token_head_offset = pid_token * hc_mult * hidden_size + pid_head * hidden_size\n    hs_base = hidden_states_ptr + token_head_offset\n    k_base = k_ptr + token_head_offset\n    out_base = output_ptr + token_head_offset\n    \n    # V is shared across heads\n    v_base = v_ptr + pid_token * hidden_size\n    \n    # Weight fused for this head\n    w_base = weight_fused_ptr + pid_head * hidden_size\n    \n    # Initialize accumulators\n    sum_x2 = 0.0\n    sum_k2 = 0.0\n    sum_xwk = 0.0\n    \n    # First pass: compute reduction stats with large block size\n    for d_start in range(0, hidden_size, BLOCK_SIZE_D):\n        d_offs = d_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE_D)\n        mask = d_offs < hidden_size\n        \n        # Load data as bf16, convert to float32\n        x = tl.load(hs_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        k = tl.load(k_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        w = tl.load(w_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        \n        # Fused multiply-add\n        sum_x2 += tl.sum(x * x, axis=0)\n        sum_k2 += tl.sum(k * k, axis=0)\n        sum_xwk += tl.sum(x * w * k, axis=0)\n    \n    # Compute rstd values\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 / hidden_size + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 / hidden_size + eps)\n    \n    # Compute dot product (normalized) for gate computation\n    dot_normalized = sum_xwk * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    \n    # Apply gate: sigmoid(sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)))\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(dot_normalized)\n    clamped_dot = tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value)\n    sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(clamped_dot)\n    signed_sqrt = tl.where(dot_normalized >= 0, sqrt_dot, -sqrt_dot)\n    gate = tl.sigmoid(signed_sqrt)\n    \n    # Save intermediates if requested\n    if save_for_backward:\n        tl.store(dot_out_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, sum_xwk)\n        tl.store(gate_score_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, gate)\n        tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, rstd_k)\n    \n    # Second pass: compute output\n    for d_start in range(0, hidden_size, BLOCK_SIZE_D):\n        d_offs = d_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE_D)\n        mask = d_offs < hidden_size\n        \n        # Load data\n        x = tl.load(hs_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        v = tl.load(v_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        \n        # Compute output: x + gate * v\n        out = x + gate * v\n        \n        # Store as bf16\n        tl.store(out_base + d_offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # v is shared across heads\n\n    Returns:\n        (output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k)\n        When save_for_backward is False, the last four are None and only `output`\n        is required to be correct.\n        When True, dot=raw_dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k are (num_tokens, hc_mult)\n        float32 tensors.\n    \"\"\"\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    \n    # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # Ensure contiguous\n    hidden_states = hidden_states.contiguous()\n    k = k.contiguous()\n    v = v.contiguous()\n    weight_fused = weight_fused.contiguous()\n    \n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n    \n    # Allocate outputs\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot_out = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot_out = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    \n    # Use maximum block size for best memory coalescing\n    BLOCK_SIZE_D = min(hidden_size, 2048)\n    \n    # Grid: one program per (token, head)\n    grid = (num_tokens, hc_mult)\n    \n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states,\n        k,\n        v,\n        weight_fused,\n        output,\n        dot_out,\n        gate_score,\n        rstd_x,\n        rstd_k,\n        num_tokens=num_tokens,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D=BLOCK_SIZE_D,\n        num_warps=16,\n        num_stages=6,\n    )\n    \n    return output, dot_out, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n"},"output":"Wrote file successfully.","metadata":{"diagnostics":{},"filepath":"/app/engram_triton.py","exists":true,"truncated":false},"title":"app/engram_triton.py","time":{"start":1784533782541,"end":1784533782544}},"id":"prt_f7e804226001himTUXRPzSWQrM","sessionID":"ses_081861573ffewpFS5uHIUjBEpO","messageID":"msg_f7e803a77001SYKJMLKhN8325V"}}

Weight fused for this head\n        w_base = weight_fused_ptr + pid_head * hidden_size\n        \n        # Initialize accumulators\n        sum_x2 = 0.0\n        sum_k2 = 0.0\n        sum_xwk = 0.0\n        \n        # First pass: compute reduction stats\n        for d_start in range(0, hidden_size, BLOCK_SIZE_D):\n            d_offs = d_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE_D)\n            mask = d_offs < hidden_size\n            \n            x = tl.load(hs_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            k = tl.load(k_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            w = tl.load(w_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            \n            sum_x2 += tl.sum(x * x, axis=0)\n            sum_k2 += tl.sum(k * k, axis=0)\n            sum_xwk += tl.sum(x * w * k, axis=0)\n        \n        # Apply gate\n        abs_dot = tl.abs(dot_normalized)\n        clamped_dot = tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value)\n        sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(clamped_dot)\n        signed_sqrt = tl.where(dot_normalized >= 0, sqrt_dot, -sqrt_dot)\n        gate = tl.sigmoid(signed_sqrt)\n        \n        # Save intermediates if requested\n        if save_for_backward:\n            tl.store(dot_out_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, sum_xwk)\n            tl.store(gate_score_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, gate)\n            tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, rstd_x)\n            tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + pid_token * hc_mult + pid_head, rstd_k)\n        \n        # Second pass: compute output\n        for d_start in range(0, hidden_size, BLOCK_SIZE_D):\n            d_offs = d_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE_D)\n            mask = d_offs < hidden_size\n            \n            x = tl.load(hs_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            v = tl.load(v_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            \n            out = x + gate * v\n            tl.store(out_base + d_offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # v is shared across heads\n\n    Returns:\n        (output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k)\n        When save_for_backward is False, the last four are None and only `output`\n        is required to be correct.\n        When True, dot=raw_dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k are (num_tokens, hc_mult)\n        float32 tensors.\n    \"\"\"\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    \n    # Ensure contiguous\n    hidden_states = hidden_states.contiguous()\n    k = k.contiguous()\n    v = v.contiguous()\n    weight_fused = weight_fused.contiguous()\n    \n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n    \n    # Allocate outputs\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot_out = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot_out = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    \n    # Use full hidden_size as block size for maximum coalescing\n    BLOCK_SIZE_D = hidden_size\n    BLOCK_SIZE_H = 4  # Process all 4 heads together\n    \n    # Grid: (num_tokens, num_head_blocks)\n    num_head_blocks = (hc_mult + BLOCK_SIZE_H - 1) // BLOCK_SIZE_H\n    grid = (num_tokens, num_head_blocks)\n    \n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states,\n        k,\n        v,\n        weight_fused,\n        output,\n        dot_out,\n        gate_score,\n        rstd_x,\n        rstd_k,\n        num_tokens=num_tokens,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D=BLOCK_SIZE_D,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_H=BLOCK_SIZE_H,\n        num_warps=16,\n        num_stages=8,\n    )\n    \n    return output, dot_out, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n"},"output":"Wrote file successfully.","metadata":{"diagnostics":{},"filepath":"/app/engram_triton.py","exists":true,"truncated":false},"title":"app/engram_triton.py","time":{"start":1784534110441,"end":1784534110445}},"id":"prt_f7e8544bf001p6B6jnXC3DIEe9","sessionID":"ses_081861573ffewpFS5uHIUjBEpO","messageID":"msg_f7e853a49001nBoXmVp670Kdk8"}}

Weight fused for this head\n        w_base = weight_fused_ptr + pid_head * hidden_size\n        \n        # Initialize accumulators\n        sum_x2 = 0.0\n        sum_k2 = 0.0\n        sum_xwk = 0.0\n        \n        # First pass: compute reduction stats\n        for d_start in range(0, hidden_size, BLOCK_SIZE_D):\n            d_offs = d_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE_D)\n            mask = d_offs < hidden_size\n            \n            x = tl.load(hs_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            k = tl.load(k_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            w = tl.load(w_base + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n            \n            sum_x2 += tl.sum(x * x, axis=0)\n            sum_k2 += tl.sum(k * k, axis=0)\n            sum_xwk += tl.sum(x * w * k, axis=0)\n        \n        # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # Allocate outputs\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot_out = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot_out = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    \n    # Optimized for AMD MI350:\n    # - Full hidden dimension block size for maximum memory coalescing\n    # - Process all heads together to share v data\n    # - 8 warps (512 threads) for good occupancy on AMD\n    # - 4 stages for optimal memory latency hiding\n    BLOCK_SIZE_D = hidden_size\n    BLOCK_SIZE_H = hc_mult  # Process all heads together\n    \n    # Grid: (num_tokens, num_head_blocks)\n    num_head_blocks = (hc_mult + BLOCK_SIZE_H - 1) // BLOCK_SIZE_H\n    grid = (num_tokens, num_head_blocks)\n    \n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states,\n        k,\n        v,\n        weight_fused,\n        output,\n        dot_out,\n        gate_score,\n        rstd_x,\n        rstd_k,\n        num_tokens=num_tokens,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_D=BLOCK_SIZE_D,\n        BLOCK_SIZE_H=BLOCK_SIZE_H,\n        num_warps=8,\n        num_stages=4,\n    )\n    \n    return output, dot_out, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n"},"output":"Wrote file successfully.","metadata":{"diagnostics":{},"filepath":"/app/engram_triton.py","exists":true,"truncated":false},"title":"app/engram_triton.py","time":{"start":1784534208369,"end":1784534208373}},"id":"prt_f7e86bfb9001tHeDsf0ZKg4Yfq","sessionID":"ses_081861573ffewpFS5uHIUjBEpO","messageID":"msg_f7e86b60b001E03L68XvNgeNhL"}}
